 kshetrarakshan bhi doum darje kaa rahaa or team india ne kuch aasaan kaich bhi tapakaae

 5 overon main ek wicket ke nuksaan par 181 genden shesh rahete hasil kar liya
 This is the second biggest defeat of the Indian team in terms of difference of balls in victory
 isse pehle bhartiya team ko 2010 main dambula main srilanka ne 209 gend shesh rahete haraaya tha

 viketon ke lihaaj se dekha jaae to srilanka ke khilaaf bharat kii yah duusari sabase badi haar bhi he
 Earlier Sri Lanka defeated India by nine wickets at Colombo in 1996
 srilanka kii kasi hui gendbaaji ke aage bhartiya sher sirf 138 ranon par dher ho gaye
 Batting first after winning the toss, the Indian team was just 33
 3 over hi maidan par tik saki
 Gautam Gambhir was the only batsman who could compete with the Sri Lankan bowlers to some extent
 unhone pari kii shuruyaat karte hue 65 ran banaae
 Gambhir made these runs with the help of four fours off 96 balls
 bharat kii ore se out hone vaale gambheer aakhri ballebaaj the
 Apart from Gambhir, only three Indian batsmen could cross the double-digit mark
 ravichandran aswin ne 21, pichley mukaable main 96 ranon kii pari khilne vaale virendra sahvaag ne 15 or captain mahendra singh dhauni ne 11 ran banaae
 For Sri Lanka, Thisara Perera and Angelo Mathews took three wickets each while Lasith Malinga took two wickets and Rangana Herath got one wicket
 perera ne aath over main keval 19 ran dekar teen wicket chatkaaye
 He broke the back by sending the top two Indian batsmen to the pavilion
 iske baad bhartiya ballebaaj kuch nahin kar sake
 Perera was awarded the title of man of the match for his brilliant performance
 bharat kii ore se rakhe gaye 139 ranon ke lakshya kaa peechha karne utari salaami ballebaaj tillakaratne dilashaan or upul tharanga kii jodi ne apni team ko shandaar shuruyaat di or pehle wicket ke liye unhone 119 ran jode
 Dilshan scored 50 runs and became the victim of Ravichandran Ashwin in the 17th over
 unhone 49 gendon kaa saamana kiya or paanch chauke lagaae
 Tharanga also batted brilliantly and scored an unbeaten 59 runs
 is dauraan unhone 60 gendon kaa saamana kiya or aath chauke lagaae
 At the other end, Dinesh Chandimal returned the unbeaten pavilion with Tharanga scoring six runs
 ballebaaji main ghatiya pradarshan ke baad bhartiya gendbaajon ne bhi niraash kiya

 srilanka ke liye anbhavi tej gendbaaj nuwan kulasekara kaa chot ke kaaran shrinkhalaa se baahar hona uske liye tagada jhatka he

 jeet main gendon ke antar ke lihaaj se yah bhartiya team kii duusari sabase badi haar he
 Earlier, the Indian team was defeated by Sri Lanka in 2010 in Dambulla with 209 balls remaining
 yahi nahin srilanka ke khilaaf bharat ko nau wicket se duusari baar haar mili he

 gambheer ne 96 gendon par chaar chaukon kii madad se ye ran banaae

 unhone chotii ke do bhartiya ballebaajon ko pavilion bhejkar qamar hi tod di
